This reduces the distance required for takeoff, and eliminates potential\n       <a href="/wiki/Crosswind" title="Crosswind">\n        crosswinds\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Marine">\n        Marine\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Marine">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Marine_weather_forecasting" title="Marine weather forecasting">\n        Marine weather forecasting\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Commercial and recreational use of waterways can be limited significantly by wind direction and speed,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ocean_surface_wave" title="Ocean surface wave">\n        wave\n       </a>\n       periodicity and heights, tides, and precipitation. These factors can each influence the safety of marine transit. Consequently, a variety of codes have been established to efficiently transmit detailed marine weather forecasts to vessel pilots via radio, for example the\n       <a href="/wiki/MAFOR" title="MAFOR">\n        MAFOR\n       </a>\n       (marine forecast).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Typical weather forecasts can be received at sea through the use of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RTTY" title="RTTY">\n        RTTY\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Navtex" title="Navtex">\n        Navtex\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Radiofax" title="Radiofax">\n        Radiofax\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Agriculture">\n        Agriculture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Agriculture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Farmer" title="Farmer">\n        Farmers\n       </a>\n       rely on weather forecasts to decide what work to do on any particular day. For example, drying\n       <a href="/wiki/Hay" title="Hay">\n        hay\n       </a>\n       is only feasible in dry weather. Prolonged periods of dryness can ruin\n       <a href="/wiki/Cotton" title="Cotton">\n        cotton\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Wheat" title="Wheat">\n        wheat\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Maize" title="Maize">\n        corn\n       </a>\n       crops. While corn crops can be ruined by drought, their dried remains can be used as a cattle feed substitute in the form of\n       <a href="/wiki/Silage" title="Silage">\n        silage\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Frost" title="Frost">\n        Frosts\n       </a>\n       and freezes play havoc with crops both during the spring and fall. For example,\n       <a href="/wiki/Peach" title="Peach">\n        peach\n       </a>\n       trees in full bloom can have their potential peach crop decimated by a spring freeze.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Orange_(fruit)" title="Orange (fruit)">\n        Orange\n       </a>\n       groves can suffer significant damage during frosts and freezes, regardless of their timing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Forestry">\n        Forestry\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Forestry">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Weather forecasting of wind, precipitations and humidity is essential for preventing and controlling\n       <a href="/wiki/Wildfire" title="Wildfire">\n        wildfires\n       </a>\n       . Different indices, like the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Forest_fire_weather_index" title="Forest fire weather index">\n         Forest fire weather index\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       and the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Haines_Index" title="Haines Index">\n         Haines Index\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , have been developed to predict the areas more at risk to experience fire from natural or human causes. Conditions for the development of harmful insects can be predicted by forecasting the evolution of weather, too.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Utility_companies">\n        Utility companies\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Utility companies">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Air_handling_unit.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="738" data-file-width="1109" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Air_handling_unit.JPG/220px-Air_handling_unit.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Air_handling_unit.JPG/330px-Air_handling_unit.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Air_handling_unit.JPG/440px-Air_handling_unit.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Air_handling_unit.JPG" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         An\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Air_handling_unit" title="Air handling unit">\n          air handling unit\n         </a>\n         is used for the heating and cooling of air in a central location (click on image for legend).\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Degree_day" title="Degree day">\n        Degree day\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Electricity and gas companies rely on weather forecasts to anticipate demand, which can be strongly affected by the weather. They use the quantity termed the degree day to determine how strong of a use there will be for heating (\n       <a href="/wiki/Heating_degree_day" title="Heating degree day">\n        heating degree day\n       </a>\n       ) or cooling (cooling degree day). These quantities are based on a daily average temperature of 65\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (18\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C). Cooler temperatures force heating degree days (one per degree Fahrenheit), while warmer temperatures force cooling degree days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n        <a href="#cite_note-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In winter, severe cold weather can cause a surge in demand as people turn up their heating.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Similarly, in summer a surge in demand can be linked with the increased use of\n       <a href="/wiki/Air_conditioning" title="Air conditioning">\n        air conditioning\n       </a>\n       systems in hot weather.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By anticipating a surge in demand, utility companies can purchase additional supplies of power or natural gas before the price increases, or in some circumstances, supplies are restricted through the use of\n       <a href="/wiki/Brownout_(electricity)" title="Brownout (electricity)">\n        brownouts\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Power_outage" title="Power outage">\n        blackouts\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_commercial_companies">\n        Other commercial companies\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Other commercial companies">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Increasingly, private companies pay for weather forecasts tailored to their needs so that they can increase their profits or avoid large losses.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       For example, supermarket chains may change the stocks on their shelves in anticipation of different consumer spending habits in different weather conditions. Weather forecasts can be used to invest in the commodity market, such as futures in oranges, corn, soybeans, and oil.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Military_applications">\n        Military applications\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Military applications">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_Kingdom_Armed_Forces">\n        United Kingdom Armed Forces\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: United Kingdom Armed Forces">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Royal Navy\n       </b>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The UK\n       <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">\n        Royal Navy\n       </a>\n       , working with the UK\n       <a href="/wiki/Met_Office" title="Met Office">\n        Met Office\n       </a>\n       , has its own specialist branch of weather observers and forecasters, as part of the Hydrographic and Meteorological (HM) specialisation, who monitor and forecast operational conditions across the globe, to provide accurate and timely weather and oceanographic information to submarines, ships and\n       <a href="/wiki/Fleet_Air_Arm" title="Fleet Air Arm">\n        Fleet Air Arm\n       </a>\n       aircraft.\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Royal_Air_Force">\n        Royal Air Force\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Royal Air Force">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       A mobile unit in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RAF" title="RAF">\n        RAF\n       </a>\n       , working with the UK\n       <a href="/wiki/Met_Office" title="Met Office">\n        Met Office\n       </a>\n       , forecasts the weather for regions in which British, allied servicemen and women are deployed. A group based at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Camp_Bastion" title="Camp Bastion">\n        Camp Bastion\n       </a>\n       provides forecasts for the British armed forces in\n       <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">\n        Afghanistan\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_Armed_Forces">\n        United States Armed Forces\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: United States Armed Forces">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="US_Navy">\n        US Navy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: US Navy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Npmoc.gif">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="101" data-file-width="100" height="101" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/30/Npmoc.gif" width="100"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Npmoc.gif" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Emblem of JTWC Joint Typhoon Warning Center\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Similar to the private sector, military weather forecasters present weather conditions to the war fighter community. Military weather forecasters provide pre-flight and in-flight weather briefs to pilots and provide real time resource protection services for military installations. Naval forecasters cover the waters and ship weather forecasts. The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">\n        United States Navy\n       </a>\n       provides a special service to both themselves and the rest of the federal government by issuing forecasts for tropical cyclones across the Pacific and Indian Oceans through their\n       <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">\n        Joint Typhoon Warning Center\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="US_Air_Force">\n        US Air Force\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Weather_forecasting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: US Air Force">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Within the United States, Air Force Weather provides weather forecasting for the Air Force and the Army.\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">\n        Air Force\n       </a>\n       forecasters cover air operations in both wartime and peacetime operations and provide\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">\n        Army\n       </a>\n       support;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">\n        United States Coast Guard\n       </a>\n       marine science technicians provide ship forecasts for ice breakers and other various operations within their realm;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and Marine forecasters provide support for ground- and air-based\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Marine_Corps" title="United States Marine Corps">\n        United States Marine Corps\n       </a>\n       operations.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All four military branches take their initial enlisted meteorology technical training at\n       <a href="/wiki/Keesler_Air_Force_Base" title="Keesler Air Force Base">\n        Keesler Air Force Base\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Military and civilian forecasters actively cooperate in analyzing, creating and critiquing weather forecast products.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a
